< username>
Brian Yoon<//username>
<text>I woke up Sunday morning to a broken irrigation pipe which resulted in having no water at all. I had to find someone who was open on Sunday and available ASAP, and I decided to call this company because I liked what other customers said about their work. I am glad I called. The receptionist was very friendly and sent someone over within thirty minutes. Larry was knowledgeable and straight to the point. He pointed out the issues, the causes that lead to the break, and what he could do to fix it. More importantly, I didn't feel like he was trying to upsell me on anything, which is something I am very cautious about as a customer. There was no pressure to buy anything at all. He spent some time to put together a few proposals and laid them all out. He explained clearly why he was proposing certain fixes in addition to the necessary repairs. <Review>After moving to Chino Hills a year ago, I knew I had to begin the hunt of finding a new barber. Over the year I tried finding other local barbershops and even continued to go to my old barber in Rancho Cucamonga.

A few months ago, I noticed Traditions Barber Shop opened up around the corner from my place. I called ahead to make a reservation, even though they accept walk-ins, which may have changed since they're a lot busier now. The place has cool decor and once you enter you'll notice all the barbers talking to their clients and being attentive to their hair. Everyone's hair looks sharp too, which is always a good sign at a barbershop.

I've had two different barbers since going to Traditions, but that's my fault for not remembering their names. One came over from a competing barbershop and the other is new to cutting, but they both gave me really good cuts. From talking to both of them, they take pride in their trade and take their time with your hair. Your sides and fades will look clean and they'll do their post to match your needs. It's cash only, so that's my one hiccup. Hopefully that changes soon.</Review>< Pictures>

< Text>
A maze of stores to choose from. Just off the 78 freeway near the 5 freeway, Pacific Coast Plaza has mostly big-box retailers like Best Buy, Dick's sporting goods, Walmart, Bed Bath and Beyond, among others. There's only one entrance and exit, which can be frustrating if the store you're going to is at the very end of the plaza. I usually come here to shop at the Best Buy, since they have a larger camera selection than normal stores.<//Text>
